<div>&lt;div id=&quot;eaembedcodecontentcustom&quot;&gt;&lt;link rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot; type=&quot;text/css&quot; href=&quot;/resource/INFAKBResource/css/bootstrap-ea.css&quot; onload=&quot;fnDoKBCssRefresh(this);&quot;/&gt;&lt;style type=&quot;text/css&quot;&gt;.expert-question{color:#0069aa}.collapsing {-webkit-transition: none;transition: none;}&lt;/style&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;container&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;masthead&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;row&quot; style=&quot;padding:10px 20px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-left&quot;&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://network.informatica.com/&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;pull-right&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse in&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Upgrade Planner for Informatica 9.6.1 (All HotFixes)&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;Informatica Upgrade Planner has been designed and created by the Informatica Global Customer Support team to provide an insight into the Informatica product upgrades.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span&gt;&lt;span&gt;This interactive self-service guide provides the information required to upgrade to Informatica 9.6.1 version from earlier versions. In this guide, you will learn:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The new features, architectural changes and steps to upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The different types of upgrade and best practices to follow during the upgrade cycle&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The upgrade process consists of the following phases:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Perform the pre-upgrade tasks/checklists&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the Informatica Server&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the Repository Service Contents&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the Informatica Client Tools&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Perform the post-upgrade tasks&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;The upgrade steps may involve additional steps based on the version you are upgrading from. To start with the upgrade, let us understand your existing implementation. This step-by-step process can be used for upgrading to all Informatica 9.6.1 HotFix versions from the earlier versions.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Note&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;It is always recommended to run the upgrade on a development environment before upgrading the production.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Select your existing Informatica version...&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#6118c170-00ae-11e5-965f-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back6118c170-00ae-11e5-965f-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;9.0.1 or Prior Versions&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#7d3a9a60-04c1-11e5-8aef-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back7d3a9a60-04c1-11e5-8aef-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;9.5.x&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#7f2d7440-04c2-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backec5048e0-03fa-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Take me to Information Upgrade Resources&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;8767cd80-0824-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Running the Service Upgrade Wizard Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text3289&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3289anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To run the &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;In the Informatica  Administrator header area, click &lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt; &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Select the objects to  upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Alternatively, specify if  you want to Automatically recycle services after upgrade. If you want to  automatically recycle services after upgrade, the &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard restarts the  services after they have been upgraded.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;If the &lt;em&gt;Dependency&lt;/em&gt; errors  exist, the &lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/em&gt; dialog box appears. Review the &lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/em&gt; and click &lt;em&gt;OK&lt;/em&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Resolve the &lt;em&gt;Dependency Errors&lt;/em&gt; and click &lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Enter the repository  login information. &lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, select the option to use the same login information for all  repositories.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;Next&lt;/em&gt;.&amp;nbsp;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;The &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard upgrades each service and displays the status and  processing details.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;When the upgrade  completes, the &lt;em&gt;Summary&lt;/em&gt; section displays the list of services and their upgrade  status.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Click each service to view the upgrade details in the &lt;em&gt;Service Details&lt;/em&gt; section.&lt;br /&gt;Alternatively, click &lt;em&gt;Save  Report&lt;/em&gt; to save the upgrade details to a file.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you do not want to save the  report, click &lt;em&gt;Save Previous Report&lt;/em&gt; the next time you launch the &lt;em&gt;Service  Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;Close&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3289Font1&quot;&gt;If you did not select to  automatically recycle services after upgrade, restart the upgraded services.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the post IDQ Services upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#7de96530-0828-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#8767cd80-0824-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back7de96530-0828-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#8767cd80-0824-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;Yes&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back8767cd80-0824-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#8767cd80-0824-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;65cdf600-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Back&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#9507a5f0-0815-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#65cdf600-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back9507a5f0-0815-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#65cdf600-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text4490&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text4490anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the domain and server  files, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Review the Operating  System specific requirements. Review the prerequisites and environment variable  configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall Informatica  B2B Data Transformation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the domain. Back  up the domain and verify database user account permissions.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the PowerCenter  repository. Back up the PowerCenter repository.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Export the Jaspersoft  resource.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare Metadata  Manager:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata  Manager warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Export, purge, and delete  business glossaries&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the Metadata  Manager service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata  Manager properties file&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the Data  Analyzer repository.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Assign roles to users and groups.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Data Analyzer  repository.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify database user account requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you are using IDQ services, review IDQ services upgrade steps before starting the upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Shut down the domain. &lt;br /&gt; You must shut down the domain before you upgrading. To shut down the domain,  stop the Informatica service process on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare to change the  node configuration. Complete the additional pre-upgrade tasks if you want to  change the node configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review the operating  system specific requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the installation  directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the keystore file  name and location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font3&quot;&gt;Domain and Server Files  Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the  domain and server files. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard  to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;The upgrade wizard installs the  Informatica files in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify  the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#58702d70-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#65cdf600-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back58702d70-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#65cdf600-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text4490&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text4490anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the domain and server  files, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Review the Operating  System specific requirements. Review the prerequisites and environment variable  configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall Informatica  B2B Data Transformation.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the domain. Back  up the domain and verify database user account permissions.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the PowerCenter  repository. Back up the PowerCenter repository.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Export the Jaspersoft  resource.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare Metadata  Manager:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata  Manager warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Export, purge, and delete  business glossaries&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Disable the Metadata  Manager service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Metadata  Manager properties file&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare the Data  Analyzer repository.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Assign roles to users and groups.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Back up the Data Analyzer  repository.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify database user account requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;If you are using IDQ services, review IDQ services upgrade steps before starting the upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Shut down the domain. &lt;br /&gt; You must shut down the domain before you upgrading. To shut down the domain,  stop the Informatica service process on each node in the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;Prepare to change the  node configuration. Complete the additional pre-upgrade tasks if you want to  change the node configuration.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Review the operating  system specific requirements.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Copy the installation  directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the keystore file  name and location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font3&quot;&gt;Domain and Server Files  Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the server installer to upgrade the  domain and server files. The server installer provides a domain upgrade wizard  to guide you through the upgrade process.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4490Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;The upgrade wizard installs the  Informatica files in the installation directory you specify. It does not modify  the files in the directory of the previous version.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back65cdf600-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#65cdf600-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#65cdf600-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;34a8bf20-0651-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Upgrade Process&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text573&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text573anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;The upgrade process involves the  following phases:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Domain and  Server files&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Application  Services&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Informatica  Client&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font5&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Domain and Server  files&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the domain and server files,  run the Informatica server installer and select the &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; option. The domain  upgrade wizard installs the server files and configures the domain. If the  domain has multiple nodes, upgrade on all the nodes.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font5&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Application Services&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;After upgrading the Domain and  Server files, log in to the &lt;em&gt;Administrator tool&lt;/em&gt; and upgrade the application  services. The &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard provides a list of all applications that  must be upgraded. It upgrades the services based on the order required by the  dependent objects.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font5&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Informatica Client&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the Informatica client, run  the Informatica client installer and select the &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; option. If the client is  installed on multiple machines, upgrade the client on all the machines.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;image1064&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the pre-installation tasks?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#34a8bf20-0651-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;f29c7000-0807-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#540b25a0-080a-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#f29c7000-0807-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back540b25a0-080a-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#f29c7000-0807-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text3831&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3831anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;To configure Kerberos authentication for  the Informatica domain at the command prompt, do the following steps:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the upgrade  was successful and the upgraded domain is working appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify the Kerberos  configuration and copy the configuration file to the Informatica  directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Create the SPNs and  keytab files that are required by the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Configure the Kerberos  authentication for the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the nodes in the  Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the client  machines.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Start the Informatica  domain and verify if that the domain runs with the Kerberos authentication appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font2&quot;&gt;Note&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;The steps provided are based on the assumption that you have  upgraded the Informatica services and clients successfully. Verify if the upgrade is complete before configuring the domain to use the Kerberos network  authentication.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Kerberos authentication is optional and is disabled by  default.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;After the Kerberos authentication is enabled for the domain, it cannot  be disabled. After the Kerberos authentication is enabled, the native users are  disabled and only the Kerberos users can be authenticated.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#3302e0f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#f29c7000-0807-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back3302e0f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#f29c7000-0807-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text3831&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3831anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;To configure Kerberos authentication for  the Informatica domain at the command prompt, do the following steps:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the upgrade  was successful and the upgraded domain is working appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify the Kerberos  configuration and copy the configuration file to the Informatica  directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Create the SPNs and  keytab files that are required by the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Configure the Kerberos  authentication for the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the nodes in the  Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the client  machines.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Start the Informatica  domain and verify if that the domain runs with the Kerberos authentication appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font2&quot;&gt;Note&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;The steps provided are based on the assumption that you have  upgraded the Informatica services and clients successfully. Verify if the upgrade is complete before configuring the domain to use the Kerberos network  authentication.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Kerberos authentication is optional and is disabled by  default.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;After the Kerberos authentication is enabled for the domain, it cannot  be disabled. After the Kerberos authentication is enabled, the native users are  disabled and only the Kerberos users can be authenticated.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New Features and Changes in 9.6.1 from 9.0.1 or Prior Releases&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;From Informatica 9.0.1 or prior release to Informatica 9.6.1, there have been multiple major changes.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Following are the key features and enhancements:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New version of IDQ that is unified with the Informatica platform through the Informatica Developer tool&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New product Informatica Data Services with support for logical data objects and unified data federation through the Informatica Developer tool&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New version of PowerCenter with enhancements for 24 x 7 operations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New version of Metadata Manager that includes Business Glossary approval workflow and various usability and performance enhancements&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Installation of Data Transformation Engine and Data Transformation Studio through the Informatica installer&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Increased Profiling functionality including filtering, identifying primary keys, foreign keys, and functional dependencies between columns in data objects&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Re-use and share Content Objects such as Token Sets, Pattern Sets, and Regular Expressions across objects. In addition, tag objects so that they can be more easily classified and searched within the repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use Data Quality for Microsoft Excel to start a mapping that reads input data from a Microsoft Excel spreadsheet&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;B2B Data Transformation is now included in Unified installer, and has new industry standard support for SEPA, FpML&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create a PowerCenter repository on Sybase ASE&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;As Platform Monitoring Enhancement, it stores and manages all run-time statistics generated from multiple Data Integration Services in a single Model Repository Service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;There is a new domain overview for large deployments. It allows Administrators to monitor the status of multiple nodes with dozens of services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Services has native Web Services capability, and you can consume externally or internally provided Web Service as part of a SQL DS, Web Service or a Data Quality mapping&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate profile metadata and Data Source connection metadata from a Data Explorer Standard Edition repository to the Model Repository that Data Explorer uses&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Specify the Informatica application client components that you want to install. For example, you can install all the application clients or a subset of application clients&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Before you install or upgrade the Informatica services, you can run the Pre-installation (i9Pi) System Check Tool to verify that the machine meets the minimum system and database requirements for the installation&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation is now available with the &lt;em&gt;CAMEO&lt;/em&gt; option&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The Content Management Service identifies the location of files that store probabilistic model data. You can set the path to the probabilistic model files on each Content Management Service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;A workflow is a graphical representation of a set of events, tasks, and decisions that define a business process. You can use the Developer tool to add objects to a workflow and to connect the objects with sequence flows.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import objects from a PowerCenter repository to a Model repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Director for Data Quality is a Web-based application that can be used to review the inappropriate and duplicate record output from an Exception transformation&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow Graphical Monitoring - Ability to view Workflow and Workflow status in Graphical format&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Out of Process ++ Execution for MRS mappings &amp;ndash; DTM (mapping) processes are pooled. Mappings are executed in a set of reusable DTM processes&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dependency Analysis for MRS objects - Ability to view upstream and downstream dependencies of objects in Developer client&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Alerts View in Developer Client - New tab in Developer Client for Connection status alerts&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Fine grained privileges for Analyst and Developer tool - Analyst and Developer tool users will need the Access Analyst and Access Developer privileges respectively to login and access associated MRS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Database based Persistence for High Availability - Before 9.6, there is hard dependency on cluster file system for storing the storage files for failover and recovery scenarios. From 9.6, it is being augmented to support database- based persistence in addition to the current Cluster File System (CFS) based persistence&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New encryption key specific to each PowerCenter server to secure the sensitive information like passwords&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;File System Security - Access to specific sensitive files are now protected by Operating System level security (Operating System level access rights)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain Audit Reports providing user/group/privilege/role/object related details&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Account lockout feature for &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;user&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;group to support more than one super user for domain&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Data Quality Address Validator, Match Transformations and Business Glossary&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New versions of the various PowerExchange products with unified administration and first-class connectivity to Neoview and Netezza. Also, various enhancements to various adaptors&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Security and search related enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New feature and enhancement to Informatica Big Data Edition&lt;/li&gt;</div>

style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are some of the points to consider while upgrading to Informatica 9.6.1 from 9.5.1 or Prior:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While performing the backup/restore steps, the post-upgrade user will lose &lt;em&gt;PCSF_RUN_LOG&lt;/em&gt; and the licensing information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While installing 9.6.1 fresh or while upgrading to 9.6.1, the &lt;em&gt;keyword&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;input is required from the user. This replaces the generic encryption key (delivered with the product) &amp;nbsp;to encrypt passwords within the server environment. This is a mandatory step and is not dependent on whether SSL/Kerberos is being used.&amp;nbsp; &lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Note:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;Keep in mind the &lt;em&gt;keyword&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;entered during the upgrade or fresh install so that even if the encryption key is &lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;lost, it could be re-generated using the keyword.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While upgrading the domain, the log events directory points to the location you specified in the previous version. While upgrading the domain with changes to the node configuration, the log events directory points to the isp/logs directory in the new installation directory. &lt;br /&gt;To use a different directory for the logs, update the &lt;em&gt;Log Directory Path&lt;/em&gt; property for the domain in the &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt; tool. You can also use &lt;em&gt;infasetup updateGatewaynode&lt;/em&gt; to update the directory. &lt;br /&gt;For example, you can configure the log events directory as the &lt;em&gt;server/infa_shared/logs&lt;/em&gt; directory in the new installation directory.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#3d5935e0-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#48e105f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back3d5935e0-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#48e105f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are some of the points to consider while upgrading to Informatica 9.6.1 from 9.5.1 or Prior:&lt;/p&gt;</div>

This is a mandatory step and is not dependent on whether SSL/Kerberos is being used.&amp;nbsp; &lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Note:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;Keep in mind the &lt;em&gt;keyword&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;entered during the upgrade or fresh install so that even if the encryption key is &lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;lost, it could be re-generated using the keyword.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While upgrading the domain, the log events directory points to the location you specified in the previous version. You can also use &lt;em&gt;infasetup updateGatewaynode&lt;/em&gt; to update the directory. &lt;br /&gt;For example, you can configure the log events directory as the &lt;em&gt;server/infa_shared/logs&lt;/em&gt; directory in the new installation directory.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>

class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;5e02b370-04c2-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#42fd1cb0-0651-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#5e02b370-04c2-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back42fd1cb0-0651-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#5e02b370-04c2-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text573&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text573anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;The upgrade process involves the  following phases:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Domain and  Server files&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Application  Services&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Informatica  Client&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font5&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Domain and Server  files&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the domain and server files,  run the Informatica server installer and select the &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; option. The domain  upgrade wizard installs the server files and configures the domain. If the  domain has multiple nodes, upgrade on all the nodes.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font5&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Application Services&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;After upgrading the Domain and  Server files, log in to the &lt;em&gt;Administrator tool&lt;/em&gt; and upgrade the application  services. The &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard provides a list of all applications that  must be upgraded. It upgrades the services based on the order required by the  dependent objects.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font5&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Informatica Client&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the Informatica client, run  the Informatica client installer and select the &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; option. If the client is  installed on multiple machines, upgrade the client on all the machines.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;image1064&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#e19def20-0f5c-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#5e02b370-04c2-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backe19def20-0f5c-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#5e02b370-04c2-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text573&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text573anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;The upgrade process involves the  following phases:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Domain and  Server files&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Application  Services&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Informatica  Client&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font5&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Domain and Server  files&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the domain and server files,  run the Informatica server installer and select the &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; option. The domain  upgrade wizard installs the server files and configures the domain. If the  domain has multiple nodes, upgrade on all the nodes.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font5&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Application Services&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;After upgrading the Domain and  Server files, log in to the &lt;em&gt;Administrator tool&lt;/em&gt; and upgrade the application  services. The &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard provides a list of all applications that  must be upgraded. It upgrades the services based on the order required by the  dependent objects.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font5&quot;&gt;Upgrading the Informatica Client&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text573Font4&quot;&gt;To upgrade the Informatica client, run  the Informatica client installer and select the &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; option. If the client is  installed on multiple machines, upgrade the client on all the machines.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;image1064&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back5e02b370-04c2-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#5e02b370-04c2-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#5e02b370-04c2-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;ec5048e0-03fa-11e5-8b26-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Upgrade Path for Upgrade from 9.1.0 to 9.6.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;If the PowerCenter 9.1.0 domain includes the Metadata Manager Service, and Metadata Manager contains the business glossaries, upgrade to 9.5.1 HotFix 4.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;For more information on upgrading to PowerCenter 9.5.1 HotFix 4, log on to &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/login/login.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica MySupport&lt;/a&gt;, and refer to the upgrade planner for 9.5.1 upgrade.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;If this Metadata Manager is not running on your current 9.1.0 installation, proceed with the upgrade process.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Do you want to view the new features in PowerCenter 9.6.1?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#809d5b30-0402-11e5-8aef-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#39fa7940-03d2-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back809d5b30-0402-11e5-8aef-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#39fa7940-03d2-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;From Informatica 9.0.1 or prior release to Informatica 9.6.1, there have been multiple major changes.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Following are the key features and enhancements:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New version of IDQ that is unified with the Informatica platform through the Informatica Developer tool&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New product Informatica Data Services with support for logical data objects and unified data federation through the Informatica Developer tool&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New version of PowerCenter with enhancements for 24 x 7 operations&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New version of Metadata Manager that includes Business Glossary approval workflow and various usability and performance enhancements&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Installation of Data Transformation Engine and Data Transformation Studio through the Informatica installer&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Increased Profiling functionality including filtering, identifying primary keys, foreign keys, and functional dependencies between columns in data objects&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Re-use and share Content Objects such as Token Sets, Pattern Sets, and Regular Expressions across objects. In addition, tag objects so that they can be more easily classified and searched within the repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use Data Quality for Microsoft Excel to start a mapping that reads input data from a Microsoft Excel spreadsheet&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;B2B Data Transformation is now included in Unified installer, and has new industry standard support for SEPA, FpML&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create a PowerCenter repository on Sybase ASE&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;As Platform Monitoring Enhancement, it stores and manages all run-time statistics generated from multiple Data Integration Services in a single Model Repository Service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;There is a new domain overview for large deployments. It allows Administrators to monitor the status of multiple nodes with dozens of services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Services has native Web Services capability, and you can consume externally or internally provided Web Service as part of a SQL DS, Web Service or a Data Quality mapping&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate profile metadata and Data Source connection metadata from a Data Explorer Standard Edition repository to the Model Repository that Data Explorer uses&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Specify the Informatica application client components that you want to install. For example, you can install all the application clients or a subset of application clients&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Before you install or upgrade the Informatica services, you can run the Pre-installation (i9Pi) System Check Tool to verify that the machine meets the minimum system and database requirements for the installation&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation is now available with the &lt;em&gt;CAMEO&lt;/em&gt; option&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The Content Management Service identifies the location of files that store probabilistic model data. You can set the path to the probabilistic model files on each Content Management Service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;A workflow is a graphical representation of a set of events, tasks, and decisions that define a business process. You can use the Developer tool to add objects to a workflow and to connect the objects with sequence flows.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Import objects from a PowerCenter repository to a Model repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Director for Data Quality is a Web-based application that can be used to review the inappropriate and duplicate record output from an Exception transformation&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow Graphical Monitoring - Ability to view Workflow and Workflow status in Graphical format&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Out of Process ++ Execution for MRS mappings &amp;ndash; DTM (mapping) processes are pooled. Mappings are executed in a set of reusable DTM processes&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dependency Analysis for MRS objects - Ability to view upstream and downstream dependencies of objects in Developer client&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Alerts View in Developer Client - New tab in Developer Client for Connection status alerts&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Fine grained privileges for Analyst and Developer tool - Analyst and Developer tool users will need the Access Analyst and Access Developer privileges respectively to login and access associated MRS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Database based Persistence for High Availability - Before 9.6, there is hard dependency on cluster file system for storing the storage files for failover and recovery scenarios. From 9.6, it is being augmented to support database- based persistence in addition to the current Cluster File System (CFS) based persistence&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New encryption key specific to each PowerCenter server to secure the sensitive information like passwords&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;File System Security - Access to specific sensitive files are now protected by Operating System level security (Operating System level access rights)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain Audit Reports providing user/group/privilege/role/object related details&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Account lockout feature for &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;user&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;group to support more than one super user for domain&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Data Quality Address Validator, Match Transformations and Business Glossary&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New versions of the various PowerExchange products with unified administration and first-class connectivity to Neoview and Netezza. Also, various enhancements to various adaptors&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Security and search related enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New feature and enhancement to Informatica Big Data Edition&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#996d7000-0402-11e5-8aef-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#39fa7940-03d2-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back996d7000-0402-11e5-8aef-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#39fa7940-03d2-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;From Informatica 9.0.1 or prior release to Informatica 9.6.1, there have been multiple major changes.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#b91afa00-0810-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#ba6dd210-080b-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backb91afa00-0810-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#ba6dd210-080b-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text4916&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text4916anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4916Font1&quot;&gt;If you plan a hardware or database  upgrade while upgrading Informatica products, Informatica 9.6.1 has the capability  to support the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a node that runs on an unsupported Operating System.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a clone of a production domain (without altering the  production environment)&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;Use the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font2&quot;&gt;Allow changes to the Node Host Name and Port Number &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;option during the Upgrade Directory  installation, to make the following key changes to the domain configuration:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Node Host Name and Port Number&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain Database Connection&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img width=&quot;100%&quot; src=&quot;https://d6ef3eb16932b7d004a5-d1dd5be5df1a66a3a617d57681ac1c81.ssl.cf2.rackcdn.com/AdavnceInstallationOptions.JPG&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;/&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To use the advanced options before upgrading, perform the following manual steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Host       </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires copying a few configuration files to the new machine before upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Database       </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires a backup and restore of domain to a new database instance before upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#48e105f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#ba6dd210-080b-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back48e105f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#ba6dd210-080b-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text4916&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text4916anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4916Font1&quot;&gt;If you plan a hardware or database  upgrade while upgrading Informatica products, Informatica 9.6.1 has the capability  to support the following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a node that runs on an unsupported Operating System.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade a clone of a production domain (without altering the  production environment)&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;Use the &lt;/span&gt;&lt;em&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font2&quot;&gt;Allow changes to the Node Host Name and Port Number &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/em&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4919Font1&quot;&gt;option during the Upgrade Directory  installation, to make the following key changes to the domain configuration:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Node Host Name and Port Number&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain Database Connection&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img width=&quot;100%&quot; src=&quot;https://d6ef3eb16932b7d004a5-d1dd5be5df1a66a3a617d57681ac1c81.ssl.cf2.rackcdn.com/AdavnceInstallationOptions.JPG&quot; alt=&quot;&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;/&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To use the advanced options before upgrading, perform the following manual steps:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Host       </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires copying a few configuration files to the new machine before upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Change Domain Database       </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Requires a backup and restore of domain to a new database instance before upgrade.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backba6dd210-080b-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#ba6dd210-080b-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#ba6dd210-080b-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;5f448250-03fe-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#ce41e240-0405-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#5f448250-03fe-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backce41e240-0405-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#5f448250-03fe-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following is the list of the major features/enhancements with 9.6.1 release:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Installation of Data Transformation Engine and Data Transformation Studio through the Informatica installer&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Increased Profiling functionality including filtering, identifying primary keys, foreign keys, and functional dependencies between columns in data objects&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Re-use and share Content Objects such as Token Sets, Pattern Sets, and Regular Expressions across objects. In addition, you can tag objects so that they can be more easily classified and searched within the repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Use Data Quality for Microsoft Excel to start a mapping that reads input data from a Microsoft Excel spreadsheet&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;B2B Data Transformation is now included in Unified installer, and has new industry standard support for SEPA, FpML&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create a PowerCenter repository on Sybase ASE&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;As Platform Monitoring Enhancement, it stores and manages all the run-time statistics generated from multiple Data Integration Services in a single Model Repository Service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;There is a new domain overview for large deployments. It allows Administrators to monitor the status of multiple nodes with dozens of services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Services has native Web Services capability allowing you to consume externally or internally the provided Web Service as part of a SQL DS, Web Service or a Data Quality mapping&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Migrate profile metadata and Data Source connection metadata from a Data Explorer Standard Edition repository to the Model Repository that Data Explorer uses&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Specify the Informatica application client components that you want to install&lt;br /&gt;For example, you can install all of the application clients or a subset of application clients.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Before you install or upgrade the Informatica services, you can run the Pre-installation (i9Pi) System Check Tool to verify that the machine meets the minimum system and database requirements for the installation&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Address Validator transformation is now available with the &lt;em&gt;CAMEO&lt;/em&gt; option&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;The Content Management Service identifies the location of files that store probabilistic model data. You can set the path to the probabilistic model files on each Content Management Service&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;A workflow is a graphical representation of a set of events, tasks, and decisions that define a business process. You can use the Developer tool to add objects to a workflow and to connect the objects with sequence flows&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;You can import objects from a PowerCenter repository to a Model repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Informatica Data Director for Data Quality is a Web-based application allowing you to review the inappropriate and duplicate record output from an Exception transformation&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow Graphical Monitoring - Ability to view Workflow and Workflow status in Graphical format.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Out of Process ++ Execution for MRS mappings &amp;ndash; DTM (mapping) processes are pooled. Mappings are executed in a set of reusable DTM processes&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dependency Analysis for MRS objects - Ability to view upstream and downstream dependencies of objects in Developer client&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Alerts View in Developer Client - New tab in Developer Client for Connection status alerts&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Fine grained privileges for Analyst and Developer tool - Analyst and Developer tool users will need the Access Analyst and Access Developer privileges respectively to login and access associated MRS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Database based Persistence for High Availability - Before 9.6, there is hard dependency on cluster file system for storing the storage files for failover and recovery scenarios. From 9.6, it is being augmented to support database- based persistence in addition to the current Cluster File System (CFS) based persistence&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New encryption key specific to each PowerCenter server to secure the sensitive information like passwords&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;File System Security - Access to specific sensitive files are now protected by the Operating System level security (Operating System level access rights)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain Audit Reports providing user/group/privilege/role/object related details&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Account lockout feature for &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;user&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;group to support more than one super user for domain&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Data Quality Address Validator, Match Transformations and Business Glossary&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New versions of the various PowerExchange products with unified administration and first-class connectivity to Neoview and Netezza. In addition, various enhancements to various adaptors&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Security and search related enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>

class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;New features/enhancements with PowerCenter 9.6.1&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Following are the new features/enhancements with PowerCenter 9.6.1:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Workflow Graphical Monitoring - Ability to view Workflow and Workflow status in a Graphical format&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Out of Process ++ Execution for MRS mappings &amp;ndash; DTM (mapping) processes are pooled. Mappings are run in a set of reusable DTM processes&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Dependency Analysis for MRS objects - Ability to view upstream and downstream dependencies of objects in Developer client&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Alerts View in Developer Client - New tab in Developer Client for Connection status alerts&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Fine grained privileges for Analyst and Developer tool - Analyst and Developer tool users will need the Access Analyst and Access Developer privileges respectively to login and access associated MRS&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Database based Persistence for High Availability - Before 9.6, there is hard dependency on cluster file system for storing the storage files for failover and recovery scenarios. From 9.6, it is being augmented to support database- based persistence in addition to the current Cluster File System (CFS) based persistence&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New encryption key specific to each PowerCenter server to secure the sensitive information such as passwords&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;File System Security - Access to specific sensitive files are now protected by Operating System level security (Operating System level access rights)&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Domain Audit Reports providing &lt;em&gt;user/group/privilege/role/object&lt;/em&gt; related details&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Account lockout feature for &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;user&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;group to support more than one super user for domain&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enhancements to Data Quality Address Validator, Match Transformations and Business Glossary&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New versions of the various PowerExchange products with unified administration and first-class connectivity to Neoview and Netezza. In addition, various enhancements to various adaptors&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Security and search related enhancements to Metadata Manager&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;New feature and enhancement to Informatica Big Data Edition&lt;/li&gt;</div>

href=&quot;#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#31424a80-03ff-11e5-951e-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;540b25a0-080a-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#ba6dd210-080b-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#540b25a0-080a-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backba6dd210-080b-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#540b25a0-080a-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are some of the points to consider while upgrading to Informatica 9.6.1 from 9.5.1 or Prior:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While performing the backup/restore steps, the post-upgrade user will lose &lt;em&gt;PCSF_RUN_LOG&lt;/em&gt; and the licensing information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While installing 9.6.1 fresh or while upgrading to 9.6.1, the &lt;em&gt;keyword&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;input is required from the user. This replaces the generic encryption key (delivered with the product) &amp;nbsp;to encrypt passwords within the server environment. This is a mandatory step and is not dependent on whether SSL/Kerberos is being used.&amp;nbsp; &lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Note:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;Keep in mind the &lt;em&gt;keyword&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;entered during the upgrade or fresh install so that even if the encryption key is &lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;lost, it could be re-generated using the keyword.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While upgrading the domain, the log events directory points to the location you specified in the previous version. While upgrading the domain with changes to the node configuration, the log events directory points to the isp/logs directory in the new installation directory. &lt;br /&gt;To use a different directory for the logs, update the &lt;em&gt;Log Directory Path&lt;/em&gt; property for the domain in the &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt; tool. You can also use &lt;em&gt;infasetup updateGatewaynode&lt;/em&gt; to update the directory. &lt;br /&gt;For example, you can configure the log events directory as the &lt;em&gt;server/infa_shared/logs&lt;/em&gt; directory in the new installation directory.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#3d5935e0-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#540b25a0-080a-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back3d5935e0-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#540b25a0-080a-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;p&gt;The following are some of the points to consider while upgrading to Informatica 9.6.1 from 9.5.1 or Prior:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While performing the backup/restore steps, the post-upgrade user will lose &lt;em&gt;PCSF_RUN_LOG&lt;/em&gt; and the licensing information.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While installing 9.6.1 fresh or while upgrading to 9.6.1, the &lt;em&gt;keyword&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;input is required from the user. This replaces the generic encryption key (delivered with the product) &amp;nbsp;to encrypt passwords within the server environment. This is a mandatory step and is not dependent on whether SSL/Kerberos is being used.&amp;nbsp; &lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Note:&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;nbsp;Keep in mind the &lt;em&gt;keyword&lt;/em&gt;&amp;nbsp;entered during the upgrade or fresh install so that even if the encryption key is &lt;span&gt; &lt;/span&gt;lost, it could be re-generated using the keyword.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;While upgrading the domain, the log events directory points to the location you specified in the previous version. While upgrading the domain with changes to the node configuration, the log events directory points to the isp/logs directory in the new installation directory. &lt;br /&gt;To use a different directory for the logs, update the &lt;em&gt;Log Directory Path&lt;/em&gt; property for the domain in the &lt;em&gt;Administrator&lt;/em&gt; tool. You can also use &lt;em&gt;infasetup updateGatewaynode&lt;/em&gt; to update the directory. &lt;br /&gt;For example, you can configure the log events directory as the &lt;em&gt;server/infa_shared/logs&lt;/em&gt; directory in the new installation directory.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; <div>&lt;div class=&quot;WordSection1&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;&lt;span&gt;Informatica platform consists of a server component, and one or more client components. Informatica provides separate installers to upgrade the Informatica services and clients.&lt;/span&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;If the installed product version cannot be upgraded to Informatica 9.6.1, upgrade to a supported version.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p class=&quot;MsoNormal&quot;&gt;To identify the current installed Informatica product version, click &lt;em&gt;Help&lt;/em&gt; in Informatica Administrator &amp;gt; &lt;em&gt;About Informatica Administrator&lt;/em&gt; in the Informatica Administrator header area.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
