<div>&lt;p&gt;If this Metadata Manager is not running on your current 9.1.0 installation, proceed with the upgrade process.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backa1b7f9f0-0403-11e5-8aef-bc764e11861e&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a1b7f9f0-0403-11e5-8aef-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#a1b7f9f0-0403-11e5-8aef-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;c1698950-0816-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Application Services pre-upgrade checklist&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text4423&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text4423anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the Application Services, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Configure POSIX  Asynchronous I/O. &lt;br /&gt;If you install Informatica on IBM AIX, make POSIX Asynchronous  I/O available on any node where you want to run a PowerCenter Integration  Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Configure Informatica  environment variables.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Configure locale  environment variables, and verify if that the locale setting is compatible with the  code page for the repository.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Clear the browser  cache.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To update the node configuration, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Install the database  client software.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the environment  variables.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify that a graphics  display server is available.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update port numbers.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the location of  the node backup directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the keystore file  name and location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure PowerExchange  Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font2&quot;&gt;Application Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Some service versions require a service  upgrade. Use the service upgrade wizard to upgrade services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;You must upgrade the Metadata Manager  Service. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font2&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font2&quot;&gt;Informatica Client Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the client installer to upgrade the  client tools. The client tools are installed in the installation directory you  specify. The client installer configures the newly installed client tools with  the same settings as the previous version.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;Would you like to view the post-upgrade steps?&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#a3d327f0-0818-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#c1698950-0816-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backa3d327f0-0818-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#c1698950-0816-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; href=&quot;#9c65da70-081e-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#f29a4f50-0816-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back9c65da70-081e-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#f29a4f50-0816-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text4484&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text4484anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;After upgrading the domain, server  files, application services, and client files, complete the following post upgrade tasks:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure LDAP  connectivity. &lt;br /&gt;The default maximum size for user import is set to 1000. Increase  the value if you have more than 1000 users.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update ODBC data  sources. The Informatica installation includes new DataDirect ODBC drivers.  Re-create each ODBC data source to use the new drivers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the log  events directory is appropriate. To use a different directory for the logs, update  the Log Directory Path property for the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;If you exported business  glossaries from Metadata Manager, import the glossaries into the Analyst  tool.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Complete the following  post upgrade tasks for each Metadata Manager Service:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the Metadata  Manager properties file to include any customization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the Metadata  Manager Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create business glossary  resources based on the business glossaries that you imported into the Analyst  tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall and reinstall  the Metadata Manager Agent after configuring the Metadata Manager  Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update the Reporting and  Dashboards Service properties file and upgrade to Jaspersoft 4.2.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#115cafc0-0824-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#f29a4f50-0816-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back115cafc0-0824-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#f29a4f50-0816-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text4484&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text4484anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;After upgrading the domain, server  files, application services, and client files, complete the following post upgrade tasks:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Configure LDAP  connectivity. &lt;br /&gt;The default maximum size for user import is set to 1000. Increase  the value if you have more than 1000 users.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update ODBC data  sources. The Informatica installation includes new DataDirect ODBC drivers.  Re-create each ODBC data source to use the new drivers.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the log  events directory is appropriate. To use a different directory for the logs, update  the Log Directory Path property for the domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;If you exported business  glossaries from Metadata Manager, import the glossaries into the Analyst  tool.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Complete the following  post upgrade tasks for each Metadata Manager Service:&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the Metadata  Manager properties file to include any customization.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable the Metadata  Manager Service.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Create business glossary  resources based on the business glossaries that you imported into the Analyst  tool.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Uninstall and reinstall  the Metadata Manager Agent after configuring the Metadata Manager  Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4484Font1&quot;&gt;Update the Reporting and  Dashboards Service properties file and upgrade to Jaspersoft 4.2.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; <div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text838Font1&quot;&gt;Informatica How-To Library (H2L)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;3302e0f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Back&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#f29c7000-0807-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#3302e0f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backf29c7000-0807-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#3302e0f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text267&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To upgrade the domain and the repositories, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font3&quot;&gt;Upgrade the Domain.&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font1&quot;&gt;Run the installer to upgrade  the domain. If the domain contains multiple nodes, upgrade a gateway node  before you upgrade the worker nodes.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrade the PowerCenter  Components.&lt;br /&gt;To upgrade all the repositories in the domain:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Log in to Informatica Administrator.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt;, and select &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;The &lt;em&gt;Upgrade Wizard&lt;/em&gt; will list all the repositories in the domain that require an upgrade.&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Select the services that you want to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the Post-upgrade tasks.&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the upgrade of the first gateway node.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;After upgrading the first gateway node, verify if that upgrade was successful before upgrading the other nodes in the domain.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Update plug-ins.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font1&quot;&gt;Update the repository with the latest plug-in registration files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the client.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the installer to upgrade the clients.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#27cb05a0-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#3302e0f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back27cb05a0-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#3302e0f0-0f5d-11e5-bb35-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text267&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To upgrade the domain and the repositories, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font3&quot;&gt;Upgrade the Domain.&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font1&quot;&gt;Run the installer to upgrade  the domain. If the domain contains multiple nodes, upgrade a gateway node  before you upgrade the worker nodes.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrade the PowerCenter  Components.&lt;br /&gt;To upgrade all the repositories in the domain:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Log in to Informatica Administrator.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt;, and select &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;The &lt;em&gt;Upgrade Wizard&lt;/em&gt; will list all the repositories in the domain that require an upgrade.&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Select the services that you want to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the Post-upgrade tasks.&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the upgrade of the first gateway node.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;After upgrading the first gateway node, verify if that upgrade was successful before upgrading the other nodes in the domain.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Update plug-ins.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font1&quot;&gt;Update the repository with the latest plug-in registration files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the client.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the installer to upgrade the clients.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#ebac66d0-0823-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#115cafc0-0824-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backebac66d0-0823-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#115cafc0-0824-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text3909&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3909anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3909Font1&quot;&gt;Use the &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard to  upgrade services from IDQ 9.0.1, 9.1, 9.5.x and 9.6.0 to Informatica DQ 9.6.1. The &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard provides the following options:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade multiple services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable services before the upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Display upgraded services in a list along with services that  require an upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been  upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard from the &lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt; menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3292&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3292anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font0&quot;&gt;Before y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;ou upgrade the Domain and Server files, perform the  following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.5.1, 9.5.x or 9.6.0 to IDQ 9.6.1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the following: </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Model Repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiling Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Reference Data Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Staging Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Human Task Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.1.0 to 9.6.1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the following: </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Model Repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiling Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Staging Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>

href=&quot;#f29a4f50-0816-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#9507a5f0-0815-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backf29a4f50-0816-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6').attr('href', '#9507a5f0-0815-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text4423&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text4423anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the Application Services, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Configure POSIX  Asynchronous I/O. &lt;br /&gt;If you install Informatica on IBM AIX, make POSIX Asynchronous  I/O available on any node where you want to run a PowerCenter Integration  Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Configure Informatica  environment variables.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Configure locale  environment variables, and verify if that the locale setting is compatible with the  code page for the repository.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Clear the browser  cache.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To update the node configuration, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Install the database  client software.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the environment  variables.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify that a graphics  display server is available.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update port numbers.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the location of  the node backup directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the keystore file  name and location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure PowerExchange  Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font2&quot;&gt;Application Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Some service versions require a service  upgrade. Use the service upgrade wizard to upgrade services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;You must upgrade the Metadata Manager  Service. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font2&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font2&quot;&gt;Informatica Client Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the client installer to upgrade the  client tools. The client tools are installed in the installation directory you  specify. The client installer configures the newly installed client tools with  the same settings as the previous version.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#65cdf600-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#9507a5f0-0815-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back65cdf600-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#9507a5f0-0815-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text4423&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text4423anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Before upgrading the Application Services, complete the following pre-upgrade tasks:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Configure POSIX  Asynchronous I/O. &lt;br /&gt;If you install Informatica on IBM AIX, make POSIX Asynchronous  I/O available on any node where you want to run a PowerCenter Integration  Service.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Configure Informatica  environment variables.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Configure locale  environment variables, and verify if that the locale setting is compatible with the  code page for the repository.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;Clear the browser  cache.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To update the node configuration, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Install the database  client software.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure the environment  variables.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify that a graphics  display server is available.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update port numbers.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the location of  the node backup directory.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Update the keystore file  name and location.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Configure PowerExchange  Adapters.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font2&quot;&gt;Application Service Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Some service versions require a service  upgrade. Use the service upgrade wizard to upgrade services.&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font1&quot;&gt;You must upgrade the Metadata Manager  Service. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font2&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text4423Font2&quot;&gt;Informatica Client Upgrade&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;Use the client installer to upgrade the  client tools. The client tools are installed in the installation directory you  specify. The client installer configures the newly installed client tools with  the same settings as the previous version.&lt;/p&gt;</div>

class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;1b86e110-0823-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;IDQ Services Upgrade Process&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text3909&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3909anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3909Font1&quot;&gt;Use the &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard to  upgrade services from IDQ 9.0.1, 9.1, 9.5.x and 9.6.0 to Informatica DQ 9.6.1. The &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard provides the following options:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade multiple services&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Enable services before the upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Display upgraded services in a list along with services that  require an upgrade&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Save the current or previous upgrade report&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Automatically restart the services after they have been  upgraded&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Access the &lt;em&gt;Service Upgrade&lt;/em&gt; wizard from the &lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt; menu in the header area&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;div id=&quot;text3292&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3292anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font0&quot;&gt;Before y&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;ou upgrade the Domain and Server files, perform the  following:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.5.1, 9.5.x or 9.6.0 to IDQ 9.6.1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the following: </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Model Repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiling Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Reference Data Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Staging Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Human Task Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3292Font1&quot;&gt;IDQ 9.1.0 to 9.6.1&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Prepare the following: </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Model Repository&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Profiling Warehouse&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Staging Database&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/div&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text284Font1&quot;&gt;Getting Started Guide&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text284Font2&quot;&gt;Informatica provides Getting Started  Guides for Informatica installation or upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text284Font2&quot;&gt;Refer to these guides to know  about database names and connection strings, user accounts, and port numbers,  that you need when you install/upgrade Informatica 9.6.1.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text284Font2&quot;&gt;You can access the Getting Started Guides  from the &lt;em&gt;Product Documentation&lt;/em&gt; page on &lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/login/login.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica&amp;nbsp;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/login/login.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;MySupport&lt;/a&gt;,&lt;span class=&quot;text284Font2&quot;&gt;&amp;nbsp;or by  installing the Informatica documentation set.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text286Font1&quot;&gt;Informatica Knowledge Base&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text286Font2&quot;&gt;Access the Informatica Knowledge  Base through &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://mysupport.informatica.com/login/login.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;Informatica MySupport&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text286Font2&quot;&gt;. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;li&gt;Find answers to frequently asked questions,  technical white papers, and technical tips&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text286Font4&quot;&gt;Informatica Multimedia Knowledge  Base&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text838Font1&quot;&gt;Informatica How-To Library (H2L)&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text838Font2&quot;&gt;Access the Informatica How-To Library at &lt;/span&gt;&lt;a&gt;MySupport&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text838Font2&quot;&gt;. The How-To  Library is a collection of resources explaining more about Informatica  products and features. It includes articles and interactive demonstrations that  provide solutions to common issues, compare features and behaviour, and guides  you through performing specific real-world tasks in Informatica 9.6.1.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>

<div>&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;back57a31670-082b-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#57a31670-082b-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#57a31670-082b-11e5-99c9-bc764e1116a6').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;b64b7990-0800-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;Yes&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;list-group&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;list-group-item expert-question&quot;&gt;&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#f29c7000-0807-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#b64b7990-0800-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#backf29c7000-0807-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').attr('href', '#b64b7990-0800-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text267&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To upgrade the domain and the repositories, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font3&quot;&gt;Upgrade the Domain.&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font1&quot;&gt;Run the installer to upgrade  the domain. If the domain contains multiple nodes, upgrade a gateway node  before you upgrade the worker nodes.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrade the PowerCenter  Components.&lt;br /&gt;To upgrade all the repositories in the domain:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Log in to Informatica Administrator.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt;, and select &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;The &lt;em&gt;Upgrade Wizard&lt;/em&gt; will list all the repositories in the domain that require an upgrade.&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Select the services that you want to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the Post-upgrade tasks.&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the upgrade of the first gateway node.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;After upgrading the first gateway node, verify if that upgrade was successful before upgrading the other nodes in the domain.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Update plug-ins.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font1&quot;&gt;Update the repository with the latest plug-in registration files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the client.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the installer to upgrade the clients.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;a class=&quot;list-group-item&quot; href=&quot;#27cb05a0-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e&quot; data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#b64b7990-0800-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);$('#back27cb05a0-0f5d-11e5-890d-bc764e11861e').attr('href', '#b64b7990-0800-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd');&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right btn-xs&quot; style=&quot;padding-right:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text267&quot;&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;To upgrade the domain and the repositories, do the following:&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font3&quot;&gt;Upgrade the Domain.&lt;/span&gt; </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font1&quot;&gt;Run the installer to upgrade  the domain. If the domain contains multiple nodes, upgrade a gateway node  before you upgrade the worker nodes.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Upgrade the PowerCenter  Components.&lt;br /&gt;To upgrade all the repositories in the domain:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Log in to Informatica Administrator.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Click &lt;em&gt;Manage&lt;/em&gt;, and select &lt;em&gt;Upgrade&lt;/em&gt;.&lt;br /&gt;The &lt;em&gt;Upgrade Wizard&lt;/em&gt; will list all the repositories in the domain that require an upgrade.&amp;nbsp;&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Select the services that you want to upgrade.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Complete the Post-upgrade tasks.&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Verify the upgrade of the first gateway node.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;After upgrading the first gateway node, verify if that upgrade was successful before upgrading the other nodes in the domain.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font4&quot;&gt;Update plug-ins.&amp;nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text267Font1&quot;&gt;Update the repository with the latest plug-in registration files.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Upgrade the client.  </div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;Run the installer to upgrade the clients.&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;text-center&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;btn-group&quot; style=&quot;margin-top:5px; margin-bottom:10px; &quot;&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; id=&quot;backb64b7990-0800-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#b64b7990-0800-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left guide-back&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Back&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a data-toggle=&quot;collapse&quot; href=&quot;#44c4c4b0-df3e-11e4-83f9-bc764e1116a6&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-home guide-root&quot; onClick=&quot;$('#b64b7990-0800-11e5-b3af-bc764e1028dd').collapse('hide');$('#eaembedcodecontentcustom')[0].scrollIntoView(true);&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Root&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;https://search.informatica.com/KBSearch#t=Expert&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; class=&quot;btn btn-primary glyphicon glyphicon-search guide-search&quot; style=&quot;color: #ffffff !important;text-decoration: none !important;&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;Search&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;254740f0-080a-11e5-9639-bc764e11861e&quot; class=&quot;steps collapse&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel panel-primary&quot; style=&quot;margin:5px;&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-heading&quot;&gt;&lt;h4 class=&quot;panel-title&quot;&gt;Post-installation Verification and Adding Kerberos Authentication Steps&lt;/h4&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;br/&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;panel-body&quot;&gt;&lt;div id=&quot;text3831&quot;&gt;&lt;a id=&quot;text3831anc&quot;&gt;&lt;/a&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;To configure Kerberos authentication for  the Informatica domain at the command prompt, do the following steps:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify if the upgrade  was successful and the upgraded domain is working appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Verify the Kerberos  configuration and copy the configuration file to the Informatica  directory.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Create the SPNs and  keytab files that are required by the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Configure the Kerberos  authentication for the Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the nodes in the  Informatica domain.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Update the client  machines.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Start the Informatica  domain and verify if that the domain runs with the Kerberos authentication appropriately.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ol&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font2&quot;&gt;Note&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;ul&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;The steps provided are based on the assumption that you have  upgraded the Informatica services and clients successfully. Verify if the upgrade is complete before configuring the domain to use the Kerberos network  authentication.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;Kerberos authentication is optional and is disabled by  default.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;li&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;text3831Font1&quot;&gt;After the Kerberos authentication is enabled for the domain, it cannot  be disabled. After the Kerberos authentication is enabled, the native users are  disabled and only the Kerberos users can be authenticated.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;</div>
<div>&lt;/ul&gt;</div>
